SELECT l.*,emp.Fullname as `name`,lt.ShortName,
						lt.Description as lname from leaveapplication l inner join employee emp 
						on l.ApplyEmpID_FK=emp.EmployeeID inner join `leavetype` lt on lt.LeaveID = l.LeaveTypeID_FK 
						where (date_format(l.StartDate,'%Y') = '2024' 
						or date_format(l.StartDate,'%Y') = '2024')  and emp.EmployeeID = '1'

SELECT l.*,emp.Fullname as `name`,lt.ShortName,
						lt.Description as lname from leaveapplication l inner join employee emp 
						on l.ApplyEmpID_FK=emp.EmployeeID inner join `leavetype` lt on lt.LeaveID = l.LeaveTypeID_FK 
						where (date_format(l.StartDate,'%Y') = '2024' 
						or date_format(l.StartDate,'%Y') = '2024')  and emp.EmployeeID = '3'
